# STRING - ddl_oracle_table_link

CREATE TABLE TABLE_LINK (
    LINK_ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    LINK_CODE VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    COST_CODE VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    VENDOR VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    CONTRACT VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    LINK_TYPE VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    BUCKET NUMBER NOT NULL,
    LINK_CAPACITY NUMBER NOT NULL,
    UNIT_COST_PER_MBPS_MONTHLY BINARY_DOUBLE NOT NULL,
    PO_STATUS NUMBER(1,0) NOT NULL,
    SITECODE VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    OLD_SITECODE VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    SITE_NAME VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    PHASE VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    ORIGIN VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    HO_SITECODE VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    HO_SITE_NAME VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    REGION VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    INTERNAL_REMARKS VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    CEP_EXECUTION_DATE TIMESTAMP NULL,
    POP_STATUS VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    LOCK_IN_CEP_POP_REMARKS BINARY_DOUBLE NULL,
    EXPIRE_DATE VARCHAR2(255) NULL,
    TERMINATION_DATE TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    TERMINATION_STATUS BINARY_DOUBLE NULL,
    CLUSTER_NAME_CEP BINARY_DOUBLE NULL,
    PAT_DATE TIMESTAMP NULL,
    PAT_STATUS VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    LAST_INVOICE VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    LOCK_IN_STATUS VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    FIBER_MASTER_PLAN VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    EFFECTIVE_START_TIME TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    EFFECTIVE_END_TIME TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    IS_CURRENT NUMBER NOT NULL,
    USER_ VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    UNNAMED_0 NUMBER NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT TABLE_LINK_PK PRIMARY KEY (LINK_ID)
)
